Grape Nehi
2 oz Vodka
2 oz Chambord
3 - 4 Lemon Wedges
Ice cubes
Garnish: No Garnish
Crush ice with lemon (or orange) & alcohols in a large glass. Use a strainer & pour into a cocktail glass. Garnish with a lemon wedge or salt on the glass.

Separator
1/2 oz Kahlua
1 oz Brandy
Milk
Garnish: No Garnish
Fill rocks glass with ice, add brandy, Kahlua, & milk. Shake well, return to glass.

Cafe Amore
1 ounce Cognac
1 ounce Amaretto
Coffee
Whipped cream
Garnish : Shaved Almonds
Pour the Cognac & amaretto into an Irish coffee glass. Fill with hot coffee & top with whipped cream

Anejo Highball
1 1/2 oz Anejo rum
1/2 oz Orange Curacao
2 oz Ginger Beer
1/4 oz Lime Juice
2 dashes Angostura bitters
Garnish : A lime wheel & an orange slice
Build in a highball glass & fill with ginger beer.

Hot Peppermint Patty
1 oz Peppermint Schnapps
1/2 oz Creme de Cacao (Dark)
1 tsp Creme de Menthe (Green)
5 - 8 oz Hot chocolate
1/2 - 1 oz Whipped cream
Garnish: No Garnish
Put creme de cacao & peppermint schnapps into a coffee mug & fill with hot chocolate. Top with whipped cream, & add a teaspoon of green creme de menthe.

Kool-Aid
1 1/2 oz Vodka
1/2 oz Peach Schnapps
1/2 oz Amaretto
3 oz Cranberry Juice
Garnish: No Garnish
Pour all ingredients into a highball glass filled with ice cubes. Serve, unstirred.

Creamcicle
1.5 shot of Rum (Light)
2 shots of Pina Colada Mix
4 oz Orange Soda
Garnish: No Garnish
Fill glass with ice. Combine ingredients in glass. Stir & enjoy!

Smith & Kerns
2 oz Kahlua
3 oz Milk
1 splash Soda Water
Garnish: No Garnish
Build in an iced highball glass. Top with soda, & serve.

Coffee Nudge
3/4 oz Creme de Cacao (Dark)
3/4 oz Kahlua
1/2 oz Brandy
6 - 8 oz Coffee
1 1/2 oz Whipped cream
Garnish: No Garnish
Combine all with coffee & top with whipped cream.

Cafe Caribbean
1 ounce Rum
1/2 ounce Amaretto
Coffee
Whipped cream
Garnish: Shaved Almonds
Pour the rum & amaretto into an Irish coffee glass. Fill with hot coffee, top with whipped cream

Surfer on Acid
1/2 oz Jagermeister
1/2 oz Malibu
1/2 oz Pineapple Juice
Garnish: No Garnish
Pour ingredients into a stainless steel shaker over ice & shake until completely cold. Strain into a large shot or old-fashioned glass & shoot.

Joe Collins
1 oz Scotch Whisky
2 oz Sweet & Sour Mix
Cola
Garnish: 1 cherry
Pour scotch & sweet & sour into a collins glass over ice cubes & stir well. Fill with cola & stir lightly. Top with the cherry & serve.

Jell-O Shot
1 cup Malibu
1 cup Hot Water
1 package Watermelon jell-o
Garnish: No Garnish
Mix hot water & jello. Add rum. Pour into 2 ounce cups. Serve after the jello has set.

Panty Dropper
1 oz Kahlua
1 oz Sloe gin
Half-and-half
Garnish: No Garnish
Pour kahlua & sloe gin into a tall, ice-filled glass. Fill with half & half, & serve.

Flaming Dr. Pepper
1 oz Amaretto
Bacardi 151
8 oz Beer
Garnish: No Garnish
In a shot glass, pour the Amaretto & top it off with the Bacardi 151. Light the 151 & drop into an 8oz cup of beer & then down the drink.

Mojito
1 1/2 oz. Rum (Light)
12 Mint Leaves
1/2 oz. Lime Juice
1/2 oz. Simple Syrup
Soda Water
Garnish: Mint Leaves or Lime Wheel

Agua De Tamarindo
10 oz. Dried Tamarinds (Peeled)
10 Cups of Water
1 Cup of Sugar
Garnish: No Garnish
Wash the tamarinds & soak them in 4 cups of hot water for a couple of hours. Rub the tamarinds against each other to get as much pulp as possible. Strain the mixture into a pitcher & dilute with 6 cups of cold water. Add sugar to taste.

Agua De Horchata
2 Cups of Long-Grain White Rice
7 Cups of Water
2 Cups of Milk
2 Cinnamon Sticks
1 Cup of Sugar
Garnish: No Garnish
Soak rice in 3 cups of water for a couple of hours. Crumble cinnamon & toast it on a small skillet. Strain the rice & blend it with the cinnamon & milk. Strain mixture into a pitcher & dilute it with 4 cups of water. Add sugar to taste.

Agua De Jamaica
2 Cups of Dried Hibiscus
10 Cups of Water
1 Cup of Sugar
Garnish: No Garnish
Place Hibiscus flowers in a pan with 6 cups of water. Bring to boil for a couple of minutes. Remove the pan from the heat & let it cool for 20 minutes. Strain the water into a pitcher & dilute it with 4 cups of cold water. Add sugar to taste.

Garnish: No Garnish
Blend all ingredients. Pour into a collins glass.

Flying Fairbrother
2 oz. Grapefruit Juice
1 oz. Orange Juice
1 oz. Cranberry Juice
1 tsp. Honey
Ginger Ale
Garnish: No Garnish
Pour grapefruit juice, orange juice, cranberry juice & honey into a shaker with ice. Shake & pour into a glass. Fill it with ginger ale.

Lime Tonic
1 oz. Lime Juice
Tonic Water
Garnish: Lime Wedge
Pour lime juice into a glass with ice. Fill it with tonic water.

Orangeade
4 oz. Orange Juice
1 tsp. Sugar
Water
Garnish: Orange Slice
Pour orange juice into a glass with ice. Fill it with water. Add sugar & stir.

Orangeade #2
5 oz. Orange Juice
1 oz. Lemon Juice
1 tsp. Sugar
Soda Water
Garnish: Orange Slice
Pour orange juice, lemon juice & sugar into a shaker with ice. Shake & pour into a glass. Fill it with club soda.

Peachy Hanes
2 oz. Peach Nectar
Ginger Beer
Garnish: No Garnish
Pour peach nectar into a beer mug with ice. Fill it with ginger beer.

Penzance Cocktail
2 oz. Orange Juice
Ginger Beer
Garnish: Lemon Wedge
Pour orange juice into a beer mug with ice. Fill it with ginger beer.

Pussyfoot
2 oz. Orange Juice
1 oz. Lemon Juice
splash of Grenadine
Garnish: Cherry
Pour all ingredients into a shaker with ice. Shake & strain into a chilled martini glass.

Rose & Thistle
1 Banana
4 oz. Strawberry Puree
6 oz. Milk
Garnish: No Garnish
Blend all ingredients with ice. Pour into a collins glass.

Virgin Pina Colada #2
4 oz. Pineapple Juice
4 oz. Cream of Coconut
Garnish: Pineapple Slice & Cherry
Blend all ingredients with ice. Pour into a hurricane glass.

Chi-Chi (Classic)
2 oz. Vodka
4 oz. Cream of Coconut
4 oz. Pineapple Juice
Garnish: Pineapple Slice & Cherry
Blend all ingredients with ice. Pour into a hurricane glass.

Frozen Melon Margarita
1 1/2 oz. Tequila
1 oz. Melon Liqueur
Margarita Mix
Garnish: Melon Wedge or Lime Wheel
Rub rim of a margarita glass with a lime & dip it into sugar. Blend all ingredients with ice. Pour into the margarita glass.

Frozen Blue Margarita
1 1/2 oz. Tequila
1/2 oz. Blue Curacao
Margarita Mix
Garnish: Lime Wedge or Lime Wheel
Rub rim of a margarita glass with a lime & dip it into kosher salt. Blend all ingredients with ice. Pour into the salted margarita glass.
